<rating>1<//rating>< Text>
Incredibly rude. I was berated for not making an appointment beforehand, even though nowhere on the website said by appointment only. I did try calling the week prior to confirm store hours but no one picked up the phone.

I went in to see if I could sell a few coins and get an opinion of whether another coin was worth sending in for grading. I was told unless I had bought the coins from him he had no interest in buying since the coins had little resale value. Fair enough, but he asked how I came to own them and expressed great skepticism when I told him, as if I had stolen them.

I asked for his opinion on the coin I was thinking of getting graded, he looked at it for 5 seconds without even inspecting it and told me it was fake. After I explained I had bought it from a reputable Bay Area dealer then his tune changed.

Overall, the experience was so unpleasant that a lady who was dining outside with her friends and overheard the entire conversation actually stopped me as I was leaving and referred me to another coin shop nearby.</Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
I had a great experience with Vince and Sal!  My father, a long-time coin and antique collector, recently passed away, leaving behind his beloved collection.  I wanted to start offloading some of it, so I called Falcone Coins and spoke with Vince.  He told me things to look out for on the coins to determine if they were valuable and said that I could send him a list of what I was looking to sell as well as some pictures.  I made an appointment to come in later that week and met with Vince and his father.

I came in somewhat prepared, with a list of what I had and what I thought they may be worth, based on similar eBay listings.  Vince and his dad went through each item and told me what they'd be willing to pay, with absolutely no pressure.  Don't expect their prices to match the highest prices you may see online, but keep in mind, auction sites take a large commission and entail a lot of work.  For as quick and efficient as the process was, I thought their offers were incredibly fair/generous.  I had a few pieces of gold jewelry, which Sal took the time to test and weigh to give me a fair price.  He even suggested that I keep a nice, personalized gold charm bracelet, unless I really needed the money.  I probably brought in a few too many items though, because I started to lose track of what I agreed to sell versus keep.

To my pleasant surprise though, a few weeks later, I received an e-mail from Vince to let me know that his dad spent more time looking at the coins that he bought from me and noticed that one was more valuable than he had originally noticed.  He had me come back to the shop to give me $300.  What an awesome, honest gesture!

I would recommend this place to anyone looking to sell coins, silver, jewelry, etc!  My advice is to do a little research about the stuff you have before you come in - that way you can easily accept or turn down their offers.  If you have something they don't want to buy, don't take it personally.  If you call and feel like Vince is being short on the phone, it's just because they are very busy and trying to help lots of people.  Both of the times I came in, their phone was constantly ringing, but they made sure to answer every call.  Looking forward to going back soon to sell some more things!< /Text>

< review>
It's divey, casual, and I had to swat away a large mosquito since I was sitting next to a large open window but the FOOD shined.

I got the Caldo de Camaron (Shrimp soup) and a Rebueltas Pupusa. I didn't realize the soup also came with 2 thick tortillas and a plate of mixed rice so it obviously became too much food for me.

But the important part was the soup with the huge shrimp and the cheesy pupusa, which came with a jar of pickled veggies that cut down the richness and went well with everything. It was SO satisfying. The soup was creamy, had large chunks of veggies, and juicy shrimp. Definitely a winner.

Would love to come back to try more different soups, pupusas and maybe the breakfast!</review>

< review>
Beware for those on VSP coverage.

However excellent place to get your examination, this facility does not house optometrist for your eye glasses.

What this means is that whomever on VSP coverage won't be able to get their glasses made here (although you will be met with wonderful staffs)  Further complicate the issue, most optometrist won't see you unless you get your examination done at the same time.  Meaning by mistake, if you get your examination here, you will suffer the grave consequences.

Your only option at this point is to travel to their nearest frenchise to location which "occasionally" has in house optometrist which is in Rowland heights.

And by god. All these was not explained at the front nor when I was making the appointment.
On VSP website list this facility as "premier" meaning it's all in one stop shopping. Which is not.

By not disclosing such a small detail made me waste time and money. Plus headaches.</review>

< review>
I went to this Meineke location to take advantage of an oil change special.  They got the job done for me and told me there was a problem with the emissions system, but it was too late in the day for them to investigate it.  I searched the site more on Google and saw some of the negative reviews.  Honestly, it is hard to know what to think from reviews with the mix of good and bad.  In the end I went to a Firestone location because one of the things Walter told me could be wrong is a gasket and I had some work done there, so I wanted Firestone to rule that it out.  It turned out that the muffler was broken.

I think like many people there is a concern that someone at an autoshop will try to get to you to do unnecessary work.   I am grateful to Walter for alerting me to the problem.

Ultimately, I got a recommendation to another shop with a slightly better price, and that is a bit more convenient for me.  I am one of the people that has to make dollars stretch.  However, I am definitely going to keep this Meineke in mind for future automotive needs.  I think one thing people might need to keep in mind in reading negative reviews is that people working at auto-shops can have bad days too . . .  there are times things go things can wrong.

My own experience was courteous service, and being given valuable, accurate information.  Thank you Walter and crew at Northridge, Meineke.<//review>

< text>
I went in for an oil change. They told me I needed new brakes. I previously had NO issues with my car or heard any noises other than the brake light occasionally coming on while driving. But stupidly I believed them and without a second opinion allowed them to replace my brakes. After about a day of driving I began to hear a faint noise that I assumed was another problem that they (probably falsely) told me my car had. But by the end of the day my wheels had completely locked up resulting in me almost hitting another car in a crowded parking lot.
When I called AAA to tow my car, the tow truck driver looked at my wheel and said "I hope you know how to sue people. Whoever did this to your car is stupid".  He told me they didn't tighten the caliber and the bolt became loose and FELL OFF. AAA told me that it was up to the mechanic to tow the car in situations where they are liable. He canceled the order and left me at the parking lot. I had to get a lyft home at 2AM!
I called Meineke first thing the next morning (7:30AM) and told them what happened and that they needed to send a tow truck. They didn't call me back until after 12noon! By then I had to go to work. They said they would call me by 10AM the next day.  By 10:30 the next day they still hadn't called.
When I finally called and spoke to Amado, he argued with me a lot and made it seem like the whole situation was MY fault and not theirs for incorrectly installing my brakes. He even said "You have to understand we're human we make mistakes" and blamed me for not bringing my car in sooner when the window between my first hearing the noise and the wheels locking up was like 4 hours (between 2:30-6:30pm), I was at work for most of that time, they closed at 6:30, and I thought the noise was from a different problem that his shop claimed I had.  He then tried to get me to pay for the tow truck and acted like he wasn't going to tow the car if I didn't pay for some of it.  After I told him exactly what AAA said then he finally ordered the tow truck.
When I met the tow truck driver at the lot, even he was visibly astonished at the condition of my vehicle and kept saying "why did they leave it like that".
When I got to the Meineke Amado apologized for his attitude on the phone with me that morning because he had "a lot going on".  He kept mentioning how much he had to pay for the tow truck. Like I was supposed to be thankful or something when none of this was my fault.  He should have been offering additional compensation like a refund for the completely third-rate brake job that I probably never even needed in the first place. He said he would test drive it himself. After about 2-3 hours they "fixed it" and then some very young guy is driving my car and I said "I thought Amado was going to test drive it".  Then after that Amado test drives it and claims that everything is okay.
After about 10 days I begin to hear the noise AGAIN. I take the car to a different mechanic and explain what has already transpired. The new mechanic told me that 1. The caliber was STILL loose and 2. MEINEKE PUT THE WRONG SIZED BOLT ON THE CAR AND IT WAS DAMAGING THE THREADS ON THE CALIBER!!
He said that I was lucky that he was able to salvage the threads or else he would have had to replace the whole caliber.
I feel so stupid that I let them talk me into a brake job without a second opinion. I trusted them because I had been there before and they were nice and helpful. I will NEVER GO BACK THERE AGAIN and I really think they should be shut down until they can hire a competent staff. They are PUTTING PEOPLE'S LIVES AT RISK and damaging people's vehicles.  On top of the fact they are probably misdiagnosing car problems for the sake of pocketing more cash.
I have filed a complaint with the corporate office and I really hope they can remedy this situation. This has been a terrible nightmare of an experience for me.< /text>

I have called and emailed corporate and have yet to receive a response. Avoid this place at all costs because you will have to spend more money to correct the issues they caused your car. <text>I moved to North County 9 years ago and happily found this place, it was good, 9 years ago. The place has gone down hill ever since in food quality, quantity and service only going up a steep hill in price. Today was, sad to say, definitely  my last visit. I have never received a smile here. Today was the first time I got my toast WITH breakfast instead of for desert but dang, it was burnt and really, really small. My daughters french toast was smaller than a slice of wonder bread. My complete breakfast was NOT GOOD. It took over 40 min. for us to get our food and our order was the only one for the kitchen at the time. "Regulars" seem to be treated better than the average joe as evidenced by today's regulars Buddy the bulldog and his owner whom were served immediately upon entering the restaurant. Yes, Buddy the dog was served dog food from behind the counter in the restaurant (Buddy probably ate the best of anyone there today). The current stone faced waitress whom has been there for a long time as far as I can remember, is bouncing all over the place looking busy enough yet nothing is really happening, except the dog is getting stellar service on the floor from her (we were stuck there for over an hour mainly waiting for food and the check) and with all the activity by the waitress feeding, petting the dog etc. I never once saw the waitress wash her hands!
So, a couple of flavorless eggs, cold undercooked sausage, burnt, mini, dry sourdough toast (they don't butter it for you) and mushy, starchy hashbrowns along with mini french toast, a cup of coffee, an orange juice from a carton and "dirty" service for $25.00 without so much as a thank you of even a smile?
THANKS BUT NO THANKS.</text><pictures>None<//pictures><Response>None< /Response>< GmapID>
